ثُمَّ يُقِيمُ بِمَكَّةَ حَرَامًا لِأَنَّهِ مُحْرِمُ بِالْحَجِّ فَلَا يَتَحَلَّلُ قَبْلَ الْإِثْيَانِ بِأَفْعَالِهِ وَيَطُوفُ بِالْبَيْتِ كَمَا بَدَالَهُ لِأَنَّهُ يُشْبِهُ الصَّلوةَ قَالَ عَلَيْهِ السَّلَامُ الطَّوَافُ بِالْبَيْتِ صَلوةُ وَالصَّلوةُ خَيْرٌ مَوضُوعِ فَكَذَا الطَّوَافُ إِلَّا أَنَّهُ لَا يَسْعَى عَقِيبَ هذِهِ الْأُطُوفَةِ فِي هَذِهِ الْمُدَّةِ لِأَنَّ السَّعْيَ لَا يَجِبُ فِيهِ إِلَّا مَرَّةَ وَالتَنْقُلُ بِالسَّعِى غَيْرُ مَشْرُوعِ وَيُصَلَّى لِكُلِّ أَسْبُوعِ رَكْعَتَيْنِ وَهِيَ رَكَعَنَا الطَّرَافِ عَلَى مَا بَيِّنا
ترجمہ پھر بحالت احرام مکہ المکرمہ میں ٹھہرا رہے۔ کیونکہ یہ شخص حج کا اجرام باندھنے والا ہے۔ اس لئے حج کے افعال ادا کرنے سے پہلے حلال نہیں ہوگا۔ اور جب جب اس کا جی چاہے بیت اللہ کا طواف کرتا رہے۔ کیونکہ طواف نماز کے مشابہ ہے حضور صلى الله عليه وسلم نے فرمایا ہے کہ بیت اللہ کا طواف کرنا نماز ہے اور نماز نیکی بنا کر وضع کی گئی ہے۔ پس اسی طرح طواف بھی ( خیر موضوع ہے ) مگر شخص اس مدت میں ان ( نفلی ) طوافوں کے بعد سعی نہیں کرے گا۔ کیونکہ حج میں سنی ایک ہی مرتبہ واجب ہوتی ہے اور نفلی طور پر سعی کرنا مشروع نہیں ہے او ریہ ہر سات چکر پر دو رکعت پڑھے۔ اور یہ طواف کی دورکعتیں ہیں ۔ اس بنیاد پر جو ہم بیان کر چکے ہیں ۔ تشریح صاحب قدوری فرماتے ہیں کہ طواف قدوم اور سعی سے فراغت کے بعد یہ شخص بحالت احرام مکتہ المکرمہ میں قیام کرے۔ کیونکہ اس نے حج ادا کرنے کے ارادہ سے احرام باندھا ہے۔ اس لئے بغیر افعال حج ادا کئے احرام سے نہ نکلے یعنی ایسا کوئی کام نہ کرے جس سے احرام سے باہر ہو جاتا ہے۔ البتہ اس مدت قیام میں جب جی چاہے طواف کرتا رہے۔ اس کی دلیل یہ ہے کہ طواف نماز کے مشابہ ہے۔ کیونکہ حضور صلى الله عليه وسلم نے فرمایا ہے الطَّوَافُ بِالْبَيْتِ صَلوةٌ إِلَّا أَنَّ اللَّهَ تَعَالَى اَحَلَّ فِيهِ الْمَنْطِقُ فَمَنْ نَطَقَ فِيهَ فَلَايَنْطِقُ إِلَّا بِخیر یعنی خانہ کعبہ کا طواف کرنا نماز ہے مگر اللہ تعالیٰ نے طواف کے اندر بات کرنا حلال کر دیا ہے۔ پس جو کوئی طواف کے اندر بات کرے تو نہ بولے مگر اچھی بات۔ اس حدیث سے ظاہر ہوتا ہے کہ طواف نماز کے مشابہ ہے اور نماز ایک نیک کام ہے جس کو چند مخصوص اوقات کے علاوہ ہر وقت ادا کیا جا سکتا ہے پس اسی طرح طواف بھی ہر وقت کیا جا سکتا ہے۔ ہاں اتنی بات ضرور ہے کہ اس مدت میں ان نفلی طوافوں کے بعد صفا اور مروہ کے درمیان سعی نہیں کی جائے گی۔ کیونکہ سعی فقط ایک بار واجب ہے اور وہ طواف قدوم کے بعد کی جا چکی۔ اور رہا بطور نفل سعی کرنا تو وہ مشروع نہیں ہے۔ اس لئے ایک سعی کے بعد دوبارہ بھی نہ کی جائے ۔ صاحب ہدایہ فرماتے ہیں کہ یہ نیلی طواف کرنے والا ہر سات شوط پر دورکعت نماز پڑھے۔ اور یہ دو رکعت صلوۃ طواف کہلاتی ہے جیسا کہ سابق میں حدیث گذر چکی ہے۔
Then after sa'y, he should stay in Makkah in the state of ihram because he is in ihram for Hajj, so he cannot become halal (i.e., exit ihram) until he performs the acts of Hajj. And he should perform tawaf of the House as often as he wishes, because tawaf resembles prayer. The Prophet (peace be upon him) said: 'Tawaf of the House is prayer, and prayer is the best of actions placed (by Allah).' So too is tawaf. However, he should not perform sa'y after these (nafl) tawafs during this period, because sa'y is only obligatory once, and performing sa'y as nafl is not legislated. And he should pray two rak'ahs for each seven circuits, and these are the two rak'ahs of tawaf, as we have explained. Translation: Then he stays in Makkah in the state of ihram. Because this person is in ihram for Hajj, he will not become halal before performing the acts of Hajj. And whenever he wishes, he may perform tawaf of the House. Because tawaf resembles prayer. The Prophet (peace be upon him) said: Tawaf of the House is prayer. And prayer is an act of goodness that was created (as the best). Similarly, tawaf is also (the best of actions). But the person should not perform sa'y after these (nafl) tawafs during this period. Because sa'y is only obligatory once in Hajj, and performing sa'y as nafl is not legislated. And he should pray two rak'ahs for every seven circuits, and these are the two rak'ahs of tawaf, based on what we have explained. Elaboration: Sahib al-Quduri says: After completing tawaf al-qudum and sa'y, this person should stay in Makkah in the state of ihram. Because he has entered ihram with the intention of performing Hajj. Therefore, he should not exit ihram until he performs the acts of Hajj, meaning he should not do anything that would cause him to leave ihram. However, during this period of stay, he may perform tawaf whenever he wishes. The evidence for this is that tawaf resembles prayer. Because the Prophet (peace be upon him) said: Tawaf of the House is prayer, except that Allah has made speech permissible in it. So whoever speaks in it should only speak good. This hadith shows that tawaf resembles prayer, and prayer is a good deed that can be performed at any time except specific prohibited times. Similarly, tawaf can be performed at any time. Yes, one thing is essential: during this period, after these nafl tawafs, sa'y should not be performed between Safa and Marwa. Because sa'y is only obligatory once, and that has already been performed after tawaf al-qudum. As for performing sa'y as nafl, it is not legislated. Therefore, it should not be repeated after one sa'y. Sahib al-Hidayah says: This person performing nafl tawaf should pray two rak'ahs after every seven circuits, and these two rak'ahs are called salat al-tawaf, as the hadith has been mentioned previously.
Source pages p. 334

Commentary
This passage is a ruling with proof from the Sunnah. It states that after performing the initial tawaf (tawaf al-qudum) and sa'y, the pilgrim remains in the state of ihram and does not exit until the completion of Hajj. During this waiting period in Makkah, the pilgrim may perform voluntary (nafl) tawaf as many times as desired. The justification is that tawaf resembles prayer in its virtue and permissibility: the hadith states that tawaf is like prayer, and prayer can be performed at any time. However, sa'y is not repeated after these nafl tawafs; sa'y is wajib (obligatory) only once during the entire Hajj, and performing sa'y on a voluntary basis is not legislated. Additionally, after each seven circuits of tawaf, the pilgrim should pray two rak'ahs of tawaf. This ruling emphasizes the Hanafi position that tawaf is like prayer but with permission to speak, and that sa'y cannot be repeated as a supererogatory act.

Key Terms
طواف (tawaf): Circumambulation of the Kaaba; in this context, it can be obligatory (tawaf al-qudum, tawaf al-ifadah) or voluntary (nafl).
سعی (sa'y): Walking between Safa and Marwa; wajib once per Hajj/Umrah.
نفل (nafl): Voluntary, supererogatory act of worship.

Key Terms from Source Passage

Checkpoint
What is the ruling on performing voluntary sa'y (walking between Safa and Marwa) after the obligatory sa'y has been completed?
A) It is sunnah to repeat sa'y often
B) It is permissible but not recommended
C) It is not legislated (mashru') and should not be done
D) It is wajib to repeat sa'y after each tawaf

Key Takeaway
In the Hanafi school, sa'y is wajib only once and cannot be repeated as nafl; however, nafl tawaf is permissible and encouraged during the stay in Makkah, as it resembles prayer.

The Three Khutbahs of Hajj: Timing and Inter-Madhhab Dispute
Ruling on timing of three Hajj khutbahs and dispute with Imam Zufar

Learning Objective
By the end of this lesson, you will be able to state the Hanafi dates for the three khutbahs of Hajj and explain the inter-madhhab dispute with Imam Zufar, including the thamarah al-khilaf.

Core Idea
The three khutbahs of Hajj are spaced with one-day gaps (7th, 9th, 11th) because teaching on busy ritual days is ineffective.

The khutbahs of Hajj are not just ritual sermons; they serve a critical educational purpose, teaching pilgrims the rites of Hajj. This lesson examines a dispute within the Hanafi school about the optimal timing of these khutbahs, balancing the need for instruction with the practical demands of the pilgrimage.

Guided Path
1
State the Hanafi position
The Hanafi school (Imam Abu Hanifa, Abu Yusuf, Muhammad) holds that the three khutbahs are on: 7th Dhul Hijjah (before Zuhr), 9th Dhul Hijjah (before Zuhr at Arafat), and 11th Dhul Hijjah (after Zuhr at Mina), with a full day gap between each.
The gap days are 8th (Tarwiyah) and 10th (Nahr).
2
Identify the opponent and his view
Imam Zufar (a Hanafi scholar) opines that the khutbahs should be on three consecutive days: first on 8th Dhul Hijjah (Yaum al-Tarwiyah), second on 9th (Arafah), and third on 11th (or 14th in some riwayah). He argues because these are the days of the hajj season and the gathering of pilgrims.
Zufar's view is considered a minority opinion within the Hanafi school.
3
Follow the opponent's proof
Zufar's dalil is based on the fact that these days (especially 8th, 9th, and 10th) are the peak days of hajj when all pilgrims are present, so they are the most suitable for teaching.
He prioritizes the gathering of the audience.
4
Analyse the Hanafi response
The Hanafi school responds that the purpose (maqsud) of the khutbahs is teaching (ta'lim). However, Yaum al-Tarwiyah (8th) and Yaum al-Nahr (10th) are days of active engagement (ishtighal) in rituals – going to Mina, standing at Arafat, etc. – so pilgrims would be too occupied to benefit. Therefore, delivering khutbahs on the adjacent off-days (7th, 9th, 11th) is more beneficial (anfa') and effective (anje' fi al-qulub). Moreover, this was the practice of the Prophet (saw) and Abu Bakr (ra).
The Hanafi reasoning combines a rational (maqasid) argument with a transmitted (naqli) support.
5
Determine the thamarah al-khilaf
The practical consequence is that the dates of the khutbahs differ: Hanafi mufta bihi are 7th, 9th, 11th; Zufar's opinion would be 8th, 9th, 11th (or 14th). This affects the schedule of pilgrims and the imam's planning.
The dispute is within the Hanafi school, so both views are technically Hanafi, but the mufta bihi is the spaced timing.

Source Text
⚠ Extracted via Advanced OCR ∼97% accuracy, minor errors may remain — always verify against original Arabic books
ایام حج شروع ہونے سے پہلے سات ذو الحجہ کو امام خطبہ دے اور کن احکامات سے حجاج کو آگاہ کرے قَالَ فَإِذَا كَانَ قَبْلَ يَومِ التَّرْوِيَةِ بِيَوْمٍ خَطَبَ الْإِمَامُ خُطْبَةً يُعَلِّمُ فِيهَا النَّاسَ الْخُرُوجَ إِلَى مِنِى وَالصَّلَوةُ بِعَرَفَاتِ وَالْوُقُوفُ وَ الْإِفَاصَةُ وَالْحَاصِلُ أنَّ فِى الْحَقِّ ثَلْتُ خُطَبِ أَوَّلُهَا مَا ذَكَرُنَا وَ الثَّانِيَةُ بِعَرَفَاتٍ يَوْمَ عَرَفَةَ وَ الثَّالِثَةُ يملى فِي الْيَوْمِ الْحَادِى عَشَرَ فَيَفْصِلُ بَيْنَ كُلّ خُطْبَتَيْنِ بِيَوْمٍ وَ قَالَ زُفَر يَخَطْبُ فِي ثَلَثَةِ أَيَّامٍ مُتَوَالِيَةٍ أَوَّلُهَا يَوْمَ التَّرْوِيَةِ لِأَنَّهَا أَيَّامُ الْمَوْسَم وَ مُجْتَمَعِ الْحَاجِ وَلَنَا أَنَّ الْمُقْصُودَ مِنْهَا التَّعْلِيمُ وَيَوْمُ التَّرْوِيَةِ وَيَوْمُ النَّحْرِ يَومُ اشْتِغَالِ فَكَانَ مَاذَكَرْنَا أَنْفَعُ وَ فِى الْقُلُوبِ انْجَعُ
ترجمه امام قدوری نے کہا کہ پھر جب یوم ترویہ سے ایک روز پہلے کا وقت ہو تو امام ایک خطبہ دے جس میں لوگوں کو منی کی طرف نکلنا ، عرفات میں نماز پڑھنا، وقوف عرفات اور وہاں سے روانہ ہونے کی تعلیم دے حاصل یہ ہے کہ حج میں تین خطبہ ہیں۔ اول خطبہ تو وہ جو ہم نے ذکر کیا ہے۔ اور دوسرا خطبہ یوم عرفہ میں میدان عرفات میں اور تیسرا خطبہ منی میں گیارہویں تاریخ کو۔ پس ہر دو خطبوں کے درمیان ایک دن کا فصل کرے۔ اور امام زفر نے کہا کہ پے در پے تین دن خطبہ دے۔ پہلا خطبہ یوم ترویہ میں کیونکہ یہ ایام خاص حج اور حاجیوں کے جمع ہونے کے ایام ہیں۔ اور ہماری دلیل یہ ہے کہ ان خطبوں سے مقصود افعال حج کی تعلیم ہے اور یوم ترویہ اور یوم نحر مشغولیت کے دن ہیں ۔ پس جو ہم نے ذکر کیا وہ زیادہ نافع اور دلوں میں مؤثر ہے۔ تشریح صاحب قدوری نے فرمایا ہے کہ ساتویں ذی الحجہ کو ظہر کی نماز کے بعد امام ایک خطبہ دے گا۔ جس میں وہ لوگوں کو افعال حج کی ے گا۔ مثلا منی کی طرف جانا ، میدان عرفات میں ظہر و عصر کو جمع کر کے پڑھنا، عرفات میں وقوف کرنا اور پھر وہاں سے کوچ کر کے
مزدلفہ کی طرف جانا۔ صاحب ہدایہ کہتے ہیں کہ حج کے زمانہ میں تین خطبے ہیں۔ پہلا خطبہ تو ساتویں ذی الحجہ کو نماز ظہر کے بعد اور دوسرا خطبہ نویں ذی الحجہ کو میدان عرفات میں نماز ظہر سے پہلے اور تیسرا خطبہ گیارہویں ذی الحجہ کو بعد نماز ظہر مقام منی میں ۔ پہلے اور تیسرے خطبہ میں دو خطبوں کے درمیان جلوس نہیں ہو گا۔ بلکہ فقط ایک خطبہ ہو گا۔ اور دوسرے خطبہ یعنی یوم عرفہ کو دو خطبوں کے درمیان بیٹھنا بھی ضروری ہے۔ صاحب ہدایہ نے کہا کہ ان خطبات ثلاثہ میں ایک ایک دن کا فصل ہوگا۔ یعنی پہلے اور دوسرے خطبہ کے درمیان آٹھویں ذی الحجہ کا فضل ہوگا اور دوسرے اور تیسرے کے درمیان دسویں ذی الحجہ کا فصل ہو گا۔ حضرت امام زفر فر ماتے ہیں کہ یہ تینوں خطبے مسلسل اور پے در پے ہیں۔ یعنی پہلا خطبہ آٹھویں ذی الحجہ کو دوسرا نویں ذی الحجہ کو اور تیسرا چودھویں ذی الحجہ کو ہے۔ امام زفر کی دلیل یہ ہے کہ یہ تینوں دن اوقات حج اور حاجیوں کے جمع ہونے کے ایام ہیں اس لئے انہیں ایام میں خطبہ دینا مناسب ہے۔ ہماری دلیل یہ ہے کہ ان خطبات سے حاجیوں کو افعال حج کی تعلیم دینا مقصود ہے اور آٹھویں ذی الحجہ اور دسویں ذی الحجہ ادائے افعال میں مشغول ہونے کے دن ہیں۔ اس کے برخلاف ساتویں اور نویں اور گیارہویں ذی الحجہ میں لوگوں کو قدرے فرصت ہوتی ہے۔ اس لئے ان تاریخوں میں خطبہ دینا لوگوں کے لئے نفع بخش بھی ہوگا ۔ اور دلوں میں مؤثر بھی ثابت ہوگا۔ اس کے علاوہ سرکار دو عالم صلى الله عليه وسلم اور آپ کے رفیق غار ابو بکر کا معمول بھی یہی ہے۔
Before the days of Hajj begin, on the 7th of Dhul Hijjah, the Imam gives a khutbah and informs the pilgrims about the rulings. He (al-Quduri) said: When it is one day before Yaum al-Tarwiyah (8th Dhul Hijjah), the Imam gives a khutbah in which he teaches the people about going out to Mina, praying in Arafat, the standing (wuquf), and the departure (ifadah). The conclusion is that in Hajj there are three khutbahs: the first is what we mentioned, the second is at Arafat on the day of Arafah, and the third is on the 11th day (in Mina). So he separates between each two khutbahs by one day. Imam Zufar said: He gives khutbahs on three consecutive days, the first on Yaum al-Tarwiyah because these are the days of the season (mawsim) and the gathering of the pilgrims. Our evidence is that the purpose of these khutbahs is teaching, and Yaum al-Tarwiyah and Yaum al-Nahr are days of occupation (with acts). So what we mentioned is more beneficial and more effective in hearts. Translation: Imam al-Quduri said: Then when it is one day before Yaum al-Tarwiyah, the Imam gives a khutbah in which he teaches the people about going to Mina, praying in Arafat, standing at Arafat, and leaving from there. The conclusion is that there are three khutbahs in Hajj. The first is the one we mentioned. The second khutbah is on the day of Arafah in the field of Arafat. The third khutbah is on the 11th day in Mina. So there should be a gap of one day between each two khutbahs. Imam Zufar said: He should give khutbahs on three consecutive days. The first khutbah on Yaum al-Tarwiyah because these are the days of the season and the gathering of the pilgrims. Our evidence is that the purpose of these khutbahs is teaching the acts of Hajj, and Yaum al-Tarwiyah and Yaum al-Nahr are days of engagement. So what we mentioned is more beneficial and more effective in hearts. Elaboration: Sahib al-Quduri said: On the 7th of Dhul Hijjah after Zuhr prayer, the Imam gives a khutbah in which he teaches the people the acts of Hajj, for example, going to Mina, combining Zuhr and Asr in Arafat, standing in Arafat, and then departing to Muzdalifah. Sahib al-Hidayah says: There are three khutbahs during the time of Hajj: the first khutbah is on the 7th of Dhul Hijjah after Zuhr prayer; the second khutbah is on the 9th of Dhul Hijjah in the field of Arafat before Zuhr prayer; the third khutbah is on the 11th of Dhul Hijjah after Zuhr prayer at Mina. In the first and third khutbahs, there is no sitting (juloos) between two parts; it is only one khutbah. In the second khutbah (on the day of Arafah), sitting between the two parts is necessary. Sahib al-Hidayah said: Among these three khutbahs, there is a gap of one day: between the first and second, the gap is the 8th of Dhul Hijjah; between the second and third, the gap is the 10th of Dhul Hijjah. Imam Zufar says that these three khutbahs are consecutive: the first on the 8th of Dhul Hijjah, the second on the 9th, and the third on the 14th (i.e., 11th? Actually, the commentary says 14th but that seems a mistake; the text says 11th earlier). Imam Zufar's evidence is that these three days are times of Hajj and gathering of pilgrims, so giving khutbahs on these days is appropriate. Our evidence is that the purpose of these khutbahs is to teach pilgrims the acts of Hajj, and the 8th and 10th are days of engagement in performing acts. In contrast, on the 7th, 9th, and 11th, people have some leisure time. Therefore, giving khutbahs on these dates is more beneficial and effective. Moreover, the practice of the Prophet (peace be upon him) and his companion Abu Bakr was also this (i.e., the Hanafi position).
Source pages p. 335

Commentary
This passage is an inter-madhhab dispute between the Hanafi school (represented by al-Quduri and al-Hidayah) and Imam Zufar regarding the timing of the three khutbahs of Hajj. The Hanafi position is that the first khutbah is on the 7th of Dhul Hijjah, the second on the 9th (Day of Arafah), and the third on the 11th (in Mina). There is a gap of one day between each: between 1st and 2nd is the 8th (Yaum al-Tarwiyah), and between 2nd and 3rd is the 10th (Yaum al-Nahr). Imam Zufar argues for consecutive days: 8th, 9th, and 11th (or 14th, according to the commentary, but this appears inconsistent; the text likely means 8th, 9th, and 10th? However, the comment clarifies that the third is on the 11th according to the Hanafi view, but Zufar says 8th, 9th, and 14th. There may be confusion in the commentary; the core issue is the spacing. The Hanafi reason is that the purpose of these khutbahs is education, and people are busy on the 8th and 10th with acts of Hajj, so the khutbahs are better placed on days when people have more leisure. Additionally, the practice of the Prophet and Abu Bakr is cited as evidence for the Hanafi timing.

Key Terms
خطبہ (khutbah): A sermon delivered by the Imam during Hajj to educate pilgrims about the rites.
یوم الترویہ (Yaum al-Tarwiyah): The 8th of Dhul Hijjah, the day pilgrims go to Mina and prepare for Arafah.
یوم النحر (Yaum al-Nahr): The 10th of Dhul Hijjah, the day of sacrifice (Eid al-Adha).
فصل (fasl): Gap or separation between two khutbahs, meaning an intervening day.

Key Terms from Source Passage

Checkpoint
According to the Hanafi school as presented in this text, on which dates are the three khutbahs of Hajj delivered?
A) 7th, 8th, and 9th of Dhul Hijjah
B) 7th, 9th, and 11th of Dhul Hijjah
C) 8th, 9th, and 10th of Dhul Hijjah
D) 8th, 9th, and 11th of Dhul Hijjah

Key Takeaway
The Hanafi school places the three Hajj khutbahs on 7th, 9th, and 11th Dhul Hijjah, with a one-day gap, to maximize educational benefit, following the practice of the Prophet and Abu Bakr.

The Three Khutbahs of Hajj: Timing and the Hanafi Dispute with Imam Zufar
Intra-Hanafi dispute on khutbah timing

Learning Objective
By the end of this lesson, you will be able to state the Hanafi position on the three khutbahs of Hajj and explain why Imam Zufar's view is rejected.

Core Idea
Khutbahs are spaced for teaching effectiveness, not for gathering convenience.

This passage from Al-Hidayah clarifies the timing of the three khutbahs (sermons) of Hajj. While the imam delivers these to instruct pilgrims, Imam Zufar proposed consecutive days. The Hanafi majority maintains a spaced schedule for maximum benefit.

Guided Path
1
Identify the three khutbahs
State the dates and locations of each khutbah according to the Hanafi majority: 7th Dhul Hijjah (before Tarwiyah), 9th (Arafat), 11th (Mina).
The first is given one day before Yawm al-Tarwiyah.
2
Note the one-day gap
Observe that between each pair of khutbahs there is exactly one day: 7th to 9th (gap of 8th), 9th to 11th (gap of 10th).
This spacing is intentional.
3
Understand Zufar's objection
Imam Zufar argued for consecutive days starting from Yawm al-Tarwiyah (8th, 9th, 10th) because those are the main Hajj days when pilgrims are gathered.
He prioritizes the convenience of gathering.
4
Analyze the Hanafi response
The majority counters that the purpose is teaching (ta'līm), and the 8th and 10th are busy days (yawm ishtighal), so the 7th, 9th, and 11th are more effective for learning.
Effectiveness over convenience.
5
Determine the mufta bihi
The majority view (Abu Hanifa, Abu Yusuf, Muhammad) is mufta bihi, supported by prophetic practice and the principle of benefit.
Zufar's view is marjuh.

Source Text
⚠ Extracted via Advanced OCR ∼97% accuracy, minor errors may remain — always verify against original Arabic books
قَالَ فَإِذَا كَانَ قَبْلَ يَومِ التَّرْوِيَةِ بِيَوْمٍ خَطَبَ الْإِمَامُ خُطْبَةً يُعَلِّمُ فِيهَا النَّاسَ الْخُرُوجَ إِلَى مِنِى وَالصَّلَوةَ بِعَرَفَاتِ وَالْوُقُوفَ وَ الْإِفَاضَةَ وَالْحَاصِلُ أنَّ فِى الْحَقِّ ثَلَاثُ خُطَبٍ أَوَّلُهَا مَا ذَكَرْنَا وَ الثَّانِيَةُ بِعَرَفَاتٍ يَوْمَ عَرَفَةَ وَ الثَّالِثَةُ يَخْطُبُ [؟] فِي الْيَوْمِ الْحَادِى عَشَرَ فَيَفْصِلُ بَيْنَ كُلِّ خُطْبَتَيْنِ بِيَوْمٍ وَ قَالَ زُفَرُ يَخْطُبُ فِي ثَلَاثَةِ أَيَّامٍ مُتَوَالِيَةٍ أَوَّلُهَا يَوْمَ التَّرْوِيَةِ لِأَنَّهَا أَيَّامُ الْمَوْسِمِ وَ مُجْتَمَعِ الْحَاجِ وَلَنَا أَنَّ الْمُقْصُودَ مِنْهَا التَّعْلِيمُ وَيَوْمُ التَّرْوِيَةِ وَيَوْمُ النَّحْرِ يَوْمُ اشْتِغَالٍ فَكَانَ مَا ذَكَرْنَا أَنْفَعُ وَ فِى الْقُلُوبِ أَنْجَعُ
He said: When it is one day before the Day of Tarwiyah, the imam gives a khutbah in which he teaches the people the departure to Mina, the prayer at Arafat, the standing (wuquf), and the ifadah (departure). The conclusion is that in Hajj there are three khutbahs: the first is what we mentioned, the second is at Arafat on the Day of Arafah, and the third is delivered on the eleventh day. So he separates between each two khutbahs by one day. Zufar said: He gives khutbah on three consecutive days, the first of which is the Day of Tarwiyah, because they are the days of the season and the gathering of pilgrims. Our evidence is that the purpose of them is teaching, and the Day of Tarwiyah and the Day of Nahr are days of occupation, so what we mentioned is more beneficial and more effective in the hearts.
Source pages p. 335

Commentary
This passage is an intra-Hanafi dispute regarding the timing of the three obligatory khutbahs of Hajj. The matn by al-Quduri states that the first khutbah is given on the 7th of Dhul Hijjah (one day before Yawm al-Tarwiyah), the second on the 9th (Yawm Arafah) at Arafat, and the third on the 11th in Mina. There is a one-day gap between each. Imam Zufar disagrees, holding that the khutbahs should be on three consecutive days starting from Yawm al-Tarwiyah (8th). His reasoning is that these days are the main season of Hajj when pilgrims are gathered. The Hanafi position (Abu Hanifa, Abu Yusuf, Muhammad) counters that the purpose of the khutbahs is teaching the rites, and the 8th and 10th are busy with rituals, so the 7th, 9th, and 11th are more suitable for effective instruction. The author notes that this is also the practice of the Prophet (ﷺ) and Abu Bakr.

Key Terms
خُطْبَة (khutbah): A sermon delivered by the imam to teach pilgrims the rites of Hajj.
يَوْمُ التَّرْوِيَةِ (yawm al-tarwiyah): The 8th of Dhul Hijjah, the day pilgrims traditionally prepare water and depart to Mina.

Key Terms from Source Passage

Checkpoint
In the Hanafi school, why is the first khutbah given on the 7th rather than the 8th?
A) Because the 8th is the Day of Tarwiyah which is busy.
B) Because the Prophet did it that way.
C) Because the 7th is the day before Tarwiyah.
D) All of the above.

Key Takeaway
The three Hajj khutbahs are spaced on the 7th, 9th, and 11th to maximize teaching effectiveness by avoiding the busiest ritual days.

Departure to Mina on Yawm al-Tarwiyah: Sunnah, Not Obligation
Ruling on leaving for Mina after Fajr on 8th Dhul Hijjah and staying until Fajr on 9th

Learning Objective
By the end of this lesson, you will be able to state the sunnah practice for the pilgrim on 8th Dhul Hijjah and identify when deviation is valid but makruh tanzihan.

Core Idea
Staying in Mina on the 8th is sunnah, not wajib; abandoning it is valid but disliked.

The Day of Tarwiyah (8th Dhul Hijjah) marks the beginning of the Hajj journey to Mina. The Prophet's practice provides a clear sequence, but what if a pilgrim chooses a different schedule? This passage from Al-Hidayah clarifies that while following the sunnah is best, deviating does not invalidate the Hajj — it only reduces the reward.

Guided Path
1
Identify the recommended act
Determine the specific action the text prescribes for the pilgrim after Fajr on Yawm al-Tarwiyah.
The text says: pray Fajr in Makkah, then go to Mina and stay until after Fajr on the 9th.
2
Locate the dalil
Find the proof cited for this recommended practice. It is a hadith describing the Prophet's own actions during Hajj.
The hadith is a fi'l (action) of the Prophet, which in Hanafi usul indicates sunnah, not obligation.
3
Note the consequence of deviation
What happens if a pilgrim stays in Makkah instead of Mina? The text says 'it suffices him' (yujzīhu) but he 'acts badly' (asā'a). Understand that the Hajj is valid but the pilgrim is blameworthy for abandoning the better practice.
The term 'asā'a' here indicates makruh tanzihan (disliked, not sinful).
4
Understand the ruling's level
Recognize that the text explicitly says this is a statement of preferability (al-awlawiyyah), not obligation. Departing earlier than the sunnah time is also permissible because no binding ruling is attached to this stay.
This distinguishes the ruling from wajib acts where omission would require a dam (sacrifice).

فَإِذَا صَلَّى الْفَجْرَ يَوْمَ التَّرْوِيهِ بِمَكَّةَ خَرَجَ إِلى مِني فَيُقِيمُ بِهَا حَتَّى يُصَلِّى الْفَجْرَ مِنْ يَومٍ عَرَفَة لِمَارُوِيَ أَنَّ النَّبِيَّ عَلَيْهِ السَّلَامُ صَلَّى الْفَجْرَ يَوْمَ التَّرْوِيَةِ بِمَكَّةَ فَلَمَّا طَلَعَتِ الشَّمْسُ رَاحَ إِلى مِنى فَصَلَّى بِمِنَى الظُّهَرَ وَالْعَصْرَ وَالْمَغْرِبَ وَالْعِشَاءَ وَالْفَجْرَ ثُمَّ رَاحَ إِلى عَرَفَاتِ وَ لَوْ بَاتَ بِمَكَّةَ لَيْلَةَ عَرَفَةَ وَصَلَّى بِهَا الْفَجْرَ ثُمَّ غَدَا إِلَى عَرَفَاتٍ وَمَرَّ بِمَنى أَجْزَاهُ لِأَنَّهُ لَا يَتَعَلَّقُ بِمَنى فِى هَذَا الْيَوْمِ إِقَامَةُ نُسُكٍ وَلكِنَّهُ أَسَاءَ بِتَرْكِهِ الْإِقْتِدَاءَ بِرَسُولِ اللَّهِ عَلَيْهِ السَّلَامُ قَالَ ثُمَّ يَتَوَجَّهُ إِلَى عَرَفَاتٍ فَيُقِيمُ بِهَا لِمَا رَوَيْنَا وَهَذَا بَيَانُ الْأَوْلَوِيَّةِ أَمَّا لَوْ دَفَعَ قَبْلَهُ جَازَ لِأَنَّهُ لَا يَتَعَلَّقُ بِهَذَا الْمُقَامِ حُكْمٌ قَالَ فِى الْأَصْلِ وَيَنْزِلُ بِهَا النَّاسُ لِأَنَّ الْإِنْتِبَاذَ تَجَبُّرٌ وَ الْحَالُ تَضَرُّعٌ وَالْإِجَابَةُ فِي الْجَمْعِ أَرْجَى وَقِيلَ مُرَادُهُ أَنْ لَا يَنْزِلَ عَلَى الطَّرِيقِ كَيْ لَا يُضَيِّقَ عَلَى الْمَارَّةِ
When he prays Fajr on the Day of Tarwiyah in Makkah, he goes out to Mina and stays there until he prays Fajr on the Day of Arafah, based on what is narrated that the Prophet (peace be upon him) prayed Fajr on the Day of Tarwiyah in Makkah, then when the sun rose, he went to Mina and prayed Zuhr, Asr, Maghrib, Isha, and Fajr in Mina, then went to Arafat. And if he spends the night of Arafah in Makkah and prays Fajr there, then goes early to Arafat and passes by Mina, it suffices him because there is no ritual residence (iqāmatu nusuk) attached to Mina on this day, but he acts badly by abandoning following the Messenger of Allah (peace be upon him). He said: Then he heads to Arafat and stays there based on what we narrated, and this is a statement of preferability (al-awlawiyyah). As for if he departs before that, it is permissible because no ruling is attached to this stay. He said in al-Asl: And the people descend there (with the imam) because isolation is arrogance while the situation calls for humility, and supplication in congregation is more hopeful of acceptance. And it is said his intent is that he should not descend on the road so as not to inconvenience passersby.
Source pages p. 336

Commentary
This passage gives the ruling on the pilgrim's movement on Yawm al-Tarwiyah (8th Dhul Hijjah) and Yawm Arafah (9th). The obligatory (wajib) sequence is: pray Fajr in Makkah on the 8th, then depart to Mina after sunrise (following the Prophet's sunnah), and stay in Mina until after Fajr on the 9th. Then proceed to Arafat. The proof is the hadith of the Prophet. If a pilgrim instead stays in Makkah on the night of the 9th, prays Fajr there, and then goes directly to Arafat passing through Mina, the Hajj is valid (yujzīhu) because there is no specific ritual tied to staying in Mina on the 8th; however, it is makruh tanzihan (disliked) because it abandons the better practice (khilāf al-ūlā). The author then clarifies that the ruling is about preferability, not obligation: leaving earlier (before sunrise) is also permissible. Finally, a separate ruling from al-Asl: the pilgrim should stay in Arafat with the people, not apart, because isolation suggests arrogance while the situation demands humility, and collective supplication is more likely to be accepted. Some explain this means not to camp on the road to avoid obstructing others.

Key Terms
إِقَامَةُ نُسُكٍ (iqāmatu nusuk): A ritual stay that is specifically required as part of the Hajj rites.
أَجْزَاهُ (ajzāhu): It suffices him; the Hajj is valid and no dam (sacrifice) is required.

Key Terms from Source Passage

Checkpoint
If a pilgrim stays in Makkah on the night of Arafah and goes directly to Arafat in the morning, passing through Mina, what is the ruling?
A) The Hajj is invalid and must be repeated
B) The Hajj is valid but it is makruh tanzihan
C) The Hajj is valid and it is the best practice
D) A dam (sacrifice) is required

Key Takeaway
The stay in Mina on Yawm al-Tarwiyah is a sunnah muakkadah, and departing from the sunnah is valid but disliked, as no ritual obligation (iqāmatu nusuk) attaches to it.

Departing to Mina on Yawm al-Tarwiyah: Sunnah of After Sunrise
Ruling with prophetic evidence on departure timing

Learning Objective
By the end of this lesson, you will be able to state the Hanafi ruling on the timing of departure from Makkah to Mina on the day of Tarwiyah and explain the prophetic evidence for the sunnah practice.

Core Idea
On Yawm al-Tarwiyah, the sunnah is to depart to Mina after sunrise, not immediately after Fajr.

The matn of Al-Quduri states that after Fajr on the 8th of Dhul Hijjah, the pilgrim should go to Mina and stay until Fajr of the 9th. A literal reading might suggest leaving immediately after the prayer. However, the commentary in Al-Hidayah clarifies that the sunnah, based on the Prophet's ﷺ practice, is to wait until sunrise. This lesson explores the ruling and the evidence, highlighting the importance of following the prophetic model even when a general statement might be misinterpreted.

Guided Path
1
Statement of the matn
Read Al-Quduri's text: after Fajr on Yawm al-Tarwiyah, the pilgrim goes to Mina and stays until Fajr of the 9th. Note the absence of specific timing instructions.
The matn is brief; it does not explicitly say 'immediately after Fajr'.
2
Potential misunderstanding
Identify the risk: a literal reading might imply departure immediately after Fajr. Recognize that this contradicts the prophetic practice.
The text says 'after Fajr', but does not specify a window.
3
Prophetic evidence
Examine the hadith: the Prophet ﷺ prayed Fajr in Makkah, then waited until sunrise before departing to Mina. This establishes the sunnah timing.
The hadith is an ahad hadith but its meaning is clear (qati al-dalala).
4
Final Hanafi position
Conclude: departure after sunrise is sunnah muakkadah; immediate departure is valid but makruh tanzihan (blameworthy).
Al-Marghinani in Al-Hidayah explicitly corrects the apparent reading of Quduri.

Source Text
⚠ Extracted via Advanced OCR ∼97% accuracy, minor errors may remain — always verify against original Arabic books
یوم الترویہ کے دن صبح کی نماز کے بعد منی میں اقامت اختیار کرے

فَإِذَا صَلَّى الْفَجْرَ يَوْمَ التَّرْوِيهِ بِمَكَّةَ خَرَجَ إِلى مِني فَيُقِيمُ بِهَا حَتَّى يُصَلِّى الْفَجْرَ مِنْ يَومٍ عَرَفَة لِمَارُوِيَ أَنَّ النَّبِيَّ عَلَيْهِ السَّلَامُ صَلَّى الْفَجْرَ يَوْمَ التَّرْوِيَةِ بِمَكَّةَ فَلَمَّا طَلَعَتِ الشَّمْسُ رَاحَ إِلى مِنى فَصَلَّى يمنى الظُّهَرَ وَالْعَصْرَ وَالْمَغْرِبَ وَالْعِشَاءَ وَالْفَجْرَ ثُمَّ رَاحَ إِلى عَرَفَاتِ

ترجمہ پس جب آٹھویں ذی الحجہ کو مکہ میں فجر کی نماز پڑھ چکے تو منی کی طرف نکلے۔ اور منی میں قیام کرے یہاں تک کہ نویں ذی الحجہ کو نماز فجر پڑھ لے۔ کیونکہ مروی ہے کہ رسول اکرم صلى الله عليه وسلم نے آٹھویں ذی الحجہ کو فجر کی نماز مکہ میں پڑھی ہے پھر جب آفتاب طلوع ہوا تو منیٰ کی طرف روانہ ہوئے اور منی میں ظہر، عصر، مغرب، عشاء اور فجر کی نمازیں پڑھیں پھر عرفات کی طرف روانہ ہوئے۔ تشریح افعال حج کی ترتیب بیان کرتے ہوئے صاحب قدوری نے فرمایا کہ آٹھویں ذی الحجہ کو مکتہ المکرمہ میں فجر کی نماز پڑھ کر منی چلا جائے اور منی میں نویں ذی الحجہ کی فجر تک قیام کرے حتی کہ فجر کی نماز منٹی ہی میں ادا کرے۔ قدوری کی عبارت سے ظاہر ہوتا ہے کہ آٹھویں ذی الحجہ کو فجر پڑھتے ہی منی کے لئے روانہ ہو جائے۔ حالانکہ یہ خلاف سنت ہے بلکہ سنت یہ ہے کہ آفتاب طلوع ہونے کے بعد منٹی کے لئے روانہ ہو جیسا کہ صاحب ہدایہ کی پیش کردہ حدیث سے ثابت ہوتا ہے۔ چنانچہ ارشاد ہے أَنَّ النَّبِيَّ صلى الله عليه وسلم صَلَّى الْفَجْرَ يَوْمَ الثَّرُويَّةِ بِمَكَّةَ فَلَمَّا طَلَعَتِ الشَّمْسُ رَاحَ إِلى مِنى فَصَلَّى بِمِنَى الظَّهَرَ وَالْعَصْرَ وَالْمَغْرِبَ وَالْعِشَاءَ وَالْفَجْرَ ثُمَّ رَاحَ إِلى عَرَفَاتِ
Literal: When he prays Fajr on the day of Tarwiyah in Makkah, he leaves to Mina and stays there until he prays Fajr of the day of Arafah, due to what is narrated that the Prophet ﷺ prayed Fajr on the day of Tarwiyah in Makkah, then when the sun rose he departed to Mina and prayed in Mina Zuhr, Asr, Maghrib, Isha, and Fajr, then departed to Arafat.
Source pages p. 336

Commentary
This passage states the ruling regarding the day of Tarwiyah (8th Dhul Hijjah). The matn from Quduri says to go to Mina after Fajr and stay until Fajr of the 9th. However, the commentary clarifies that this does not mean leaving immediately after Fajr; rather, the sunnah (as proven by the hadith of the Prophet) is to wait until sunrise. Thus, leaving immediately is permissible but blameworthy (khilaf al-sunnah).

Key Terms
یوم الترویہ (Yawm al-Tarwiyah): The 8th day of Dhul Hijjah, when pilgrims traditionally prepare water and go to Mina.
سنت (sunnah): A recommended practice established by the Prophet; omitting it is makruh tanzihan but the act remains valid.

Key Terms from Source Passage

Checkpoint
According to the Hanafi school, when should a pilgrim depart from Makkah to Mina on the day of Tarwiyah (8th Dhul Hijjah)?
A) Immediately after Fajr prayer
B) After sunrise, following the Prophet's practice
C) At any time during the day
D) After Zuhr prayer

Key Takeaway
The Hanafi school emphasizes that departing to Mina after sunrise on Yawm al-Tarwiyah is the sunnah, following the Prophet's practice; leaving earlier is permissible but disliked.

Staying in Makkah on the Night of Arafah and the Etiquette of Proceeding to Arafat
Ruling on permissibility but dislike of not staying in Mina on the 9th night, and the etiquette of proceeding to Arafat.

Learning Objective
By the end of this lesson, you will be able to state the ruling on spending the night of Arafah in Makkah, distinguish between valid and blameworthy practice, and explain the recommendation to stay with the congregation at Arafat.

Core Idea
Staying in Makkah on the night of Arafah is valid but blameworthy — the sunnah is to stay in Mina and proceed after sunrise.

Many pilgrims wonder whether it is acceptable to spend the night of Arafah (9th Dhul Hijjah) in Makkah instead of Mina, especially given logistical challenges. This passage from Al-Hidayah clarifies that while it is valid, it contradicts the Prophet's practice and is thus disliked. The same passage also advises on the proper etiquette of proceeding to Arafat: after Fajr in Mina, one should depart after sunrise and stay with the congregation, avoiding isolation and inconvenience to others.

Guided Path
1
Identify the two issues
The passage addresses two distinct rulings: (a) the validity of staying in Makkah on the night of Arafah, and (b) the recommended timing and manner of proceeding to Arafat. Recognize these as separate legal questions.
The first issue is about the night of Arafah; the second is about the day of Arafah.
2
Determine the hukm for staying in Makkah
The text states 'اجزاه' (it suffices) but 'اساء' (he did wrong). Identify that the act is valid (ja'iz) but blameworthy (makruh tanzihan) because it abandons the sunnah of staying in Mina.
The ruling is not that the act is invalid; rather, it is permissible but against the preferred practice.
3
Identify the dalil
The evidence for the sunnah of staying in Mina is the Prophet's practice (Sunnah ahad). Though not cited verbatim here, the text refers to what was narrated previously. Recognize that the blame attaches to omitting imitation of the Prophet.
The proof is qat'i in dalala but zanni in thubut because it is based on ahad hadith.
4
Understand 'awla' and the timing of departure
The passage clarifies that departing after sunrise is 'awla' (preferable), but departing earlier is also permissible. Distinguish between the sunnah (recommended) and mere permissibility.
Awwaliyya is a level between sunnah and mubah; omitting it is not sinful but leaves merit.
5
Apply the recommendation to stay with the congregation
Imam Muhammad advises staying with the people ('yanzilu biha al-nas') because isolation reflects arrogance in a state of humility, and congregational presence increases hope for acceptance of supplication. Also, avoid camping on the road to prevent inconvenience.
This is an adab (etiquette) ruling, not a condition of validity.

Source Text
⚠ Extracted via Advanced OCR ∼97% accuracy, minor errors may remain — always verify against original Arabic books
منی میں اقامت کی شرعی حیثیت اور عرفات کی طرف کوچ کا حکم

وَلَوْبَاتَ بِمَكَّةَ لَيْلَةَ عَرَفَة وَصَلَّى بِهَا الْفَجْرَ ثُمَّ غَدَا إِلَى عَرَفَاتٍ وَمَرَّ بِمَنيَّ أَجْزَاهُ لِأَنَّهُ لَا يَتَعَلَّقُ بِمَنى فِى هَذَا الْيَوْمِ إِقَامَةً نُسْبٍ وَلكِنَّهُ أَسَاءَ بِتَرْكِهِ الْإِفْتِدَاءَ بِرَسُولِ اللَّهِ عَلَيْهِ السَّلَامُ قَالَ ثُمَّ يَتَوَجَّهُ إِلَى عَرَفَاتٍ فَيُقِيمُ بِهَا لَمَا رَوَيْنَا وَهُذَا بَيَانُ الْأُولَوِيَّةِ أَمَّا لَوْ دَفَعَ قَبْلَهُ جَازَ لِأَنَّهُ لَا يَتَعَلَّقُ بِهَذَا الْمُقَامِ حُكْمُ قَالَ فِى الْأَصْلِ وَيُنزِلُ بِهَا النَّاسِ لأَنَّ الإِنْتِبَاذَ تَجَبُّرُ وَالْحَالُ تَضَرُّعُ وَالْإِجَابَهُ فِي الْجَمْعِ أَرْجَى وَقِيلَ مُرَادُهُ أَنْ لَا يَنْزِلَ عَلَى الطَّرِيقِ كَيْلًا يُضِيقُ عَلَى الْمَارَّةِ

ترجمہ اور اگر حاجی نے عرفہ (نویں ذی الحجہ) کی رات مکہ میں گزاری اور مکہ میں فجر کی نماز پڑھ کرعلی الصبح عرفات کو روانہ ہو گیا اور مئی سے گذرا تو اس کو کافی ہو گیا۔ اس لئے کہ اس روز منی میں کوئی نسک حج ادا کرنا متعلق نہیں ہے۔ لیکن اس نے رسول اللہ صلى الله عليه وسلم کی اقتداء کو ترک کر دینے کی وجہ سے برا کیا۔ پھر عرفات کی طرف متوجہ ہو اور عرفات میں قیام کرے اس حدیث کی وجہ سے جو ہم نے روایت کی ۔ اور یہ اولی ہونے کا بیان ہے۔ رہا یہ کہ اگر طلوع آفتاب سے پہلے عرفات کو روانہ ہوا تو جائز ہے۔ کیونکہ اس مقام میں کوئی حکم متعلق نہیں ہے۔ امام محمد نے مبسوط میں کہا اور عرفات میں لوگوں کے ساتھ اترے کیونکہ اکیلا رہنا تکبر ہے حالا تک حالت عاجزی اور تضرع کی ہے۔ اور جماعت کے ساتھ قبولیت کی زیادہ امید ہے اور کہا گیا کہ امام محمد کی مراد یہ ہے کہ راستہ پر نہ اترے تا کہ راہ چلنے والوں پر راستہ تنگ نہ ہو جائے۔

تشریح صاحب قدوری نے فرمایا ہے کہ اگر بالفرض آٹھویں ذی الحجہ کوئی نہ پہنچا بلکہ آٹھویں ذی الحجہ کا دن اور نویں تاریخ کی رات مکہ ہی میں گذاری اور نویں ذی الحجہ کو فجر کی نماز مکہ میں پڑھ کر منی سے گذرتا ہوا عرفات کے میدان میں پہنچ گیا تو یہ بھی کافی ہے۔ کیونکہ آٹھویں تاریخ کو منی میں کسی فعل حج کا ادا کرنا بظاہر مشورع معلوم نہیں ہوتا مگر چونکہ یہ عمل حضور صلى الله عليه وسلم کے عمل کے خلاف ہے اس لئے ترک اقتداء کی وجہ سے یہ شخص برائی کا مرتکب ہوگا۔
 صاحب قدوری نے اصل مسئلہ کی طرف رجوع کرتے ہوئے فرمایا کہ حاجی جب نو (۹) تاریخ کو فجر کی نماز منی میں پڑھ چکا تو اب آفتاب طلوع ہونے کے بعد عرفات چلا جائے۔ دلیل سابقہ حدیث ہے۔ لیکن یہ خیال رہے کہ طلوع آفتاب کے بعد نکلنا محض اولی ہے۔ ورنہ اگر طلوع آفتاب سے پہلے روانہ ہو گیا تو بھی جائز ہے۔ کیونکہ مقام منی میں حج کا کوئی حکم آج کے دن متعلق نہیں ہے۔ اس لئے طلوع آفتاب سے پہلے عرفات کی طرف جانے میں کوئی مضائقہ نہیں ہے۔ صاحب ہدایہ نے کہا کہ امام محمد نے مبسوط میں تحریر کیا ہے که حاجی میدان عرفات میں لوگوں کے ساتھ اترے یعنی لوگوں سے الگ نہ ہو کیونکہ لوگوں سے الگ تھلگ رہنا تکبر ہے۔ حالانکہ یہ موقع عاجزی اور تضرع کا ہے۔ دوسری بات یہ کہ جماعت کے ساتھ قبولیت دعا کی زیادہ امید ہے۔ بعض لوگوں نے کہا کہ امام محمد کی مراد یہ ہے کہ راستہ میں نہ اترے۔ کیونکہ اس صورت میں راستہ چلنے والوں کے لئے دقت پیدا ہوگی۔
Literal: And if he stays overnight in Makkah on the night of Arafah and prays Fajr there, then goes early to Arafat and passes by Mina, it suffices him because there is no ritual stay required in Mina on this day, but he does wrong by leaving the imitation of the Messenger of Allah. He said: Then he proceeds to Arafat and stays there due to what we narrated, and this is an explanation of precedence. As for if he departs before that, it is permissible because no ruling is attached to this stay. He said in al-Asl: And he should descend with the people there, because isolation is arrogance and the situation calls for humility, and acceptance in the congregation is more hoped for. And it was said his intent is that he not descend on the road so as not to narrow it for passersby.
Source pages p. 336

Commentary
This passage deals with two issues. First: if a pilgrim spends the night of the 9th in Makkah and goes directly to Arafat passing through Mina, it is valid because there is no obligatory stay in Mina on the 9th. However, it is blameworthy because it contradicts the Prophet's practice of staying in Mina. Second: regarding the stay at Arafat, it is recommended (aula) to go after sunrise, but going earlier is permissible. Additionally, Imam Muhammad advises staying with the congregation at Arafat, not isolating oneself, and not camping on the road to avoid inconvenience.

Key Terms
اولی (awla): Preferable or more meritorious; an action that is better to do but not obligatory.
اساء (asā'a): He did wrong; an action that is blameworthy but not invalidating.

Key Terms from Source Passage

Checkpoint
What is the ruling if a pilgrim spends the night of Arafah (9th) in Makkah and then goes to Arafat passing through Mina?
A) His Hajj is invalid because he missed a pillar
B) It is valid but blameworthy for abandoning the sunnah
C) It is not permissible under any circumstances
D) He must offer a sacrifice (dam) as penalty

Key Takeaway
Staying in Makkah on the night of Arafah is valid but blameworthy; the sunnah is to stay in Mina and proceed after sunrise, and at Arafat it is recommended to stay with the congregation.

The Arafah Khutbah: Before or After the Prayer?
Inter-madhhab dispute on khutbah timing at Arafat

Learning Objective
By the end of this lesson, you will be able to state the Hanafi position on the timing of the khutbah at Arafat, explain the Maliki counter-argument, and identify the practical difference (thamarah al-khilaf).

Core Idea
Hanafi: khutbah before the combined prayer; Maliki: after — the difference turns on whether it resembles Jumu'ah or Eid.

This lesson examines the dispute between the Hanafi and Maliki schools regarding the timing of the khutbah on the day of Arafah. The source passage from Al-Hidayah presents the Hanafi ruling that the imam delivers two khutbahs before combining Zuhr and Asr, and the Maliki objection that it should be after the prayer, like the Eid khutbah. We will also explore the intra-Hanafi discussion about the timing of the adhan.

Guided Path
1
Identify the issue in dispute
The core disagreement is whether the khutbah at Arafat should be delivered before or after the combined Zuhr and Asr prayer. Note that both schools agree a khutbah is delivered, but they differ on its placement.
This is an inter-madhhab dispute (Ikhtilaf bayn al-madhahib).
2
State the Hanafi position and its proof
According to the Hanafi school, the imam begins with the khutbah before the prayer. The proof is the explicit practice of the Prophet (ﷺ) as narrated in hadith. Also, the purpose of the khutbah is to teach the rites of Hajj, which is best done before the prayer.
The Hanafi position is supported by a dalil naqli (transmitted evidence).
3
State the Maliki position and its proof
Imam Malik holds that the khutbah should be after the prayer because it is a sermon and admonition, thus resembling the Eid khutbah, which is delivered after the Eid prayer.
This is a qiyas (analogy) to the Eid khutbah.
4
Analyze the Hanafi response
The Hanafi school responds that the Prophet's direct action takes precedence over analogy. Moreover, teaching the rites, which include the prayer itself, is best accomplished before the prayer so that the pilgrims can perform the combined prayer correctly.
This is an example of takhsis al-illah (limiting the effective cause) or simply prioritizing dalil naqli over qiyas.
5
Determine the thamarah al-khilaf
The practical difference is that in the Hanafi school, the khutbah will be heard before Zuhr on the day of Arafah, while in the Maliki school, it will be heard after Asr (since the two prayers are combined).
Also affects the timing of the adhan and iqamah.

Source Text
⚠ Extracted via Advanced OCR ∼97% accuracy, minor errors may remain — always verify against original Arabic books
میدان عرفات میں جمع بین الصلاتین اور خطبہ کا حکم

قَالَ وَإِذَا زَالَتِ الشَّمْسُ يُصَلّى الْإِمَامُ بِالنَّاسِ الظُّهَرَ وَالْعَصْرَ فَيَبْتَدِيُّ بِالْخُطْبَةِ فَيَخْطُبُ خُطْبَةٌ يُعَلِّمُ فِيهَا النَّاسَ الوقوفَ بِعَرَفَةَ وَالْمُرْدَ لَفَةِ وَرَى الْحِمَارِ وَالتَّحْرَ وَالْحَلْقِ وَطَوافِ الزِيَارَةِ يَخْطُبُ حُطَبَتَيْنِ يَفْصِلُ بَيْنَهُمَا بِجَلْسَةٍ كَمَا فِى الْجُمُعَةِ هَكَذَا فَعَلَهُ رَسُولُ اللهِ صلى الله عليه وسلم وَقَالَ مَالِكِ يَخْطُبُ بَعْدَ الصَّلوة لأنَّهَا خُطْبَة وَعْطٍ وَتَذْكِير فَأَشْبَهَ خُطْبَةَ الْعِيدِ وَلَنَا مَارَوَيْنَا وَلِأَنَّ الْمَقْصُودَ مِنْهَا تَعِلِيمُ الْمَنَاسِ وَالْجَمْعُ مِنْهَا وَفِى ظَاهِرِ الْمَذْهَبِ إِذًا . صَعِدَ الإِمَامُ الْمِنْبَرَ فَجَلَسَ أَذَّنَ الْمُؤَذِّنُونَ كَمَا فِى الْجُمُعَةِ وَعَنْ أَبِى يُوسُفَ أَنَّهُ يُؤَذِّنُ قَبْلَ خُرُوجِ الإِمَامِ وَعَنْهُ أنَّه يُؤَذِّنُ بَعْدَ الْخُطْبَةِ وَالصَّحِيحُ مَا ذَكَرْنَا لِأَنَّ النَّبِيَّ عَلَيْهِ السَّلَامُ لَمَّا خَرَجَ وَاسْتَوَى عَلَى نَاقَتِهِ أَذَّنَ الْمُؤَذِنُونَ بَيْنَ يَدَيْهِ وَيُقِيمُ الْمُؤذِّنُ بَعْدَ الْفَرَاغِ مِنَ الْخُطْبَةِ لأَنَّهُ أوانُ الشَّرُوعِ فِى الصَّلوة فَأَشبَهَ الْجُمْعَةَ

ترجمہ قدوری نے کہا اور جب آفتاب ڈھل جائے تو امام لوگوں کو ظہر اور عصر کی نماز پڑھائے اور خطبہ سے شروع کرے۔ چنانچہ ایسا خطبہ پڑھے جس میں لوگوں کو وقوف عرفہ ، وقوف مزدلفہ، رمی جمار قربانی کرنا ، سر منڈانا ، اور طواف زیارت کرنا سکھلائے امام دو خطبے پڑھے۔ ان دونوں کے درمیان بیٹھ ک فصل کرے جیسا کہ جمعہ میں ہے۔ ایسا ہی رسول اللہ ا نے کیا ہے۔ اور امام مالک نے فرمایا ہے کہ نماز کے بعد خطبہ پڑھے۔ کیونکہ یہ خطبہ وعظ ونصیحت ہے۔ اس لئے عید کے خطبہ کے مشابہ ہو گیا۔ اور ہماری دلیل وہ حدیث ہے جو ہم نے روایت کی ہے۔ اس لئے کہ خطبہ کا مقصود مناسک حج کی تعلیم ہے اور جمع بین الصلوتین بھی مناسک میں سے ہے اور ظاہر مذہب میں ہے کہ جب امام منبر پر چڑھ کر بیٹھے تو مؤذن لوگ اذان دیں جیسا کہ جمعہ میں ہے اور ابو یوسف سے روایت ہے کہ امام کے نکلنے سے پہلے اذان دے۔ اور ابو یوسف ہی سے مروی ہے کہ خطبہ کے بعد اذان دے اور صحیح وہ ہے جو ہم نے ذکر کیا۔ کیونکہ حضور کا جب خیمہ سے نکل
Literal: He said: When the sun declines, the imam leads the people in Zuhr and Asr, and he begins with the khutbah. He delivers a khutbah teaching the people the standing at Arafat, Muzdalifah, throwing the pebbles, sacrifice, shaving, and the tawaf al-ziyarah. He delivers two khutbahs, separating them with a sitting as in Jumu'ah. This is what the Messenger of Allah did. Malik said: He should deliver the khutbah after the prayer because it is a sermon and admonition, thus resembling the Eid khutbah. Our proof is what we narrated, and because the purpose is teaching the rituals, and combining them is from the rituals. In the apparent madhhab: When the imam ascends the minbar and sits, the mu'adhdhins give the adhan as in Jumu'ah. From Abu Yusuf: that he gives the adhan before the imam's appearance, and from him also that he gives the adhan after the khutbah. The correct is what we mentioned because when the Prophet came out and mounted his she-camel, the mu'adhdhins gave the adhan before him, and the mu'adhdhin gives the iqamah after the completion of the khutbah because it is the time of beginning the prayer, thus resembling Jumu'ah.
Source pages p. 337

Commentary
This passage rules on the Arafah khutbah and prayers. The imam combines Zuhr and Asr after the sun declines, preceded by two khutbahs (as in Jumu'ah). The khutbah content should teach the rites of Hajj. Imam Malik holds that the khutbah should be after the prayer, likening it to Eid. The Hanafi response: the Prophet's practice is evidence, and the purpose is teaching the rites, which is better before. The text also addresses the adhan timing: the apparent madhhab (Zahir al-madhhab) is that the adhan is given when the imam sits on the minbar. Abu Yusuf has two narrations (before imam's appearance or after khutbah), but the correct view is the first. The iqamah is after the khutbah, as in Jumu'ah.

Key Terms
جمع بین الصلاتین (jam' bayn al-salatayn): Combining two prayers (Zuhr and Asr) at the same time, specific to Arafat during Hajj.
ظاہر المذہب (Zahir al-madhhab): The apparent or well-known position of the Hanafi school, as transmitted in the six books of Imam Muhammad.

Key Terms from Source Passage

Checkpoint

A) After the prayer, similar to the Eid khutbah
B) Before the prayer, similar to the Jumu'ah khutbah
C) Only a single khutbah is delivered after the prayer
D) The khutbah is not required at Arafah

Key Takeaway
The Hanafi school relies on the direct practice of the Prophet for the khutbah before the combined prayer at Arafat, distinguishing it from the Eid khutbah.

Timing of Departure to Arafat on the 9th of Dhul Hijjah
Ruling on when to leave for Arafat and staying in Mina.

Learning Objective
By the end of this lesson, you will be able to state the recommended time for departing to Arafat on the 9th of Dhul Hijjah and explain why departing before sunrise is permissible yet less preferred.

Core Idea
Departing to Arafat after sunrise on the 9th is superior; earlier departure is valid but less preferable.

This lesson examines the timing of leaving for Arafat on the 9th of Dhul Hijjah. While the Prophet’s practice set a clear example of departing after sunrise, the Hanafi school emphasizes flexibility based on the absence of a specific ritual obligation at Mina on that day. The ruling balances following the Sunnah with practical ease for pilgrims.

Guided Path
1
Identify the act and its ruling
The act is departing from Mina to Arafat on the 9th. Determine the legal classification: is it wajib, sunnah, or mubah?
The text states that departing after sunrise is 'ula' (superior), meaning sunnah muakkadah, not wajib.
2
Locate the proof (dalil)
The evidence cited is the 'previous hadith' referring to the Prophet's practice. Recognize that the Hanafi school relies on this Sunnah as the basis for recommendation.
The specific hadith is not quoted here but is considered a known proof in the broader fiqh literature.
3
Understand the concept of 'ula'
'Ula' indicates a preferred action whose opposite is makruh tanzihi (disliked but not prohibited). Contrast this with fard or wajib.
This distinction is crucial: departing earlier is valid because no Hajj ritual is tied to Mina on that day.
4
Note the flexibility and consequences
The passage emphasizes that departing before sunrise is permissible. However, abandoning the preferred action (tark al-iqtida') is blameworthy.
The pilgrim should strive to follow the Prophet's example but is not sinning if they depart early due to necessity.

Source Text
⚠ Extracted via Advanced OCR ∼97% accuracy, minor errors may remain — always verify against original Arabic books
صاحب قدوری نے فرمایا ہے کہ اگر بالفرض آٹھویں ذی الحجہ کوئی نہ پہنچا بلکہ آٹھویں ذی الحجہ کا دن اور نویں تاریخ کی رات مکہ ہی میں گذاری اور نویں ذی الحجہ کو فجر کی نماز مکہ میں پڑھ کر منی سے گذرتا ہوا عرفات کے میدان میں پہنچ گیا تو یہ بھی کافی ہے۔ کیونکہ آٹھویں تاریخ کو منی میں کسی فعل حج کا ادا کرنا بظاہر مشورع معلوم نہیں ہوتا مگر چونکہ یہ عمل حضور صلى الله عليه وسلم کے عمل کے خلاف ہے اس لئے ترک اقتداء کی وجہ سے یہ شخص برائی کا مرتکب ہوگا۔ صاحب قدوری نے اصل مسئلہ کی طرف رجوع کرتے ہوئے فرمایا کہ حاجی جب نو (۹) تاریخ کو فجر کی نماز منی میں پڑھ چکا تو اب آفتاب طلوع ہونے کے بعد عرفات چلا جائے۔ دلیل سابقہ حدیث ہے۔ لیکن یہ خیال رہے کہ طلوع آفتاب کے بعد نکلنا محض اولی ہے۔ ورنہ اگر طلوع آفتاب سے پہلے روانہ ہو گیا تو بھی جائز ہے۔ کیونکہ مقام منی میں حج کا کوئی حکم آج کے دن متعلق نہیں ہے۔ اس لئے طلوع آفتاب سے پہلے عرفات کی طرف جانے میں کوئی مضائقہ نہیں ہے۔ صاحب ہدایہ نے کہا کہ امام محمد نے مبسوط میں تحریر کیا ہے که حاجی میدان عرفات میں لوگوں کے ساتھ اترے یعنی لوگوں سے الگ نہ ہو کیونکہ لوگوں سے الگ تھلگ رہنا تکبر ہے۔ حالانکہ یہ موقع عاجزی اور تضرع کا ہے۔ دوسری بات یہ کہ جماعت کے ساتھ قبولیت دعا کی زیادہ امید ہے۔ بعض لوگوں نے کہا کہ امام محمد کی مراد یہ ہے کہ راستہ میں نہ اترے۔ کیونکہ اس صورت میں راستہ چلنے والوں کے لئے دقت پیدا ہوگی۔
Sahib al-Quduri said: If by supposition someone did not reach [Mina] on the 8th of Dhul Hijjah, but rather spent the day of the 8th and the night of the 9th in Makkah, and on the 9th of Dhul Hijjah prayed Fajr in Makkah, then passing through Mina arrived at the plain of Arafat, this too is sufficient. Because performing any act of Hajj in Mina on the 8th does not appear to be legislated outwardly, but since this action is contrary to the practice of the Prophet (peace be upon him), this person will commit a wrong due to abandoning following [the Sunnah]. Sahib al-Quduri, returning to the original issue, said: When the pilgrim has prayed Fajr in Mina on the 9th, he should go to Arafat after sunrise. The evidence is the previous hadith. But note that departing after sunrise is merely superior. Otherwise, if he departs before sunrise, it is also permissible, because there is no ruling of Hajj related to Mina on this day. Therefore, there is no harm in going to Arafat before sunrise. Sahib al-Hidayah said that Imam Muhammad wrote in al-Mabsut that the pilgrim should descend in the plain of Arafat with the people, i.e., not separate from them, because isolation from people is arrogance, whereas this occasion is one of humility and supplication. Second, with the congregation there is greater hope for acceptance of supplication. Some said that Imam Muhammad's intent is that he should not descend on the road, because that would cause difficulty for passersby.
Source pages p. 337

Commentary
This passage from the Sharh discusses the rulings related to the 9th of Dhul Hijjah. It begins by quoting al-Quduri on a scenario: a pilgrim who did not stay in Mina on the 8th but instead spent the day and night in Makkah, then on the morning of the 9th prays Fajr in Makkah and travels to Arafat via Mina. This is sufficient for Hajj, but it is a shortcoming because he missed the Sunnah of staying in Mina on the 8th. The author then states the preferred action: after Fajr on the 9th in Mina, the pilgrim should wait until sunrise before departing to Arafat. This is based on the prophetic practice. However, it is only superior (ula) and not obligatory. Departing earlier is permissible because there is no specific Hajj ritual tied to Mina on that day. The passage then quotes from al-Hidayah that Imam Muhammad recommended staying with the crowd in Arafat, not isolating oneself, as humility is key. Another interpretation is to avoid stopping on the road to not block travelers. This lesson is a ruling with proof: the evidence is the Prophetic practice (hadith) indicating departure after sunrise, though the ruling allows flexibility.

Key Terms
اولی (ula): In this context, 'superior' or 'more recommended' – not obligatory or wajib.
ترک اقتداء (tark al-iqtida'): Abandoning following the Sunnah of the Prophet (peace be upon him) in the manner of performing Hajj.

Key Terms from Source Passage

Checkpoint
According to the Hanafi school, when should the pilgrim depart for Arafat on the 9th of Dhul Hijjah?
A) Immediately after Fajr prayer
B) After sunrise
C) At any time
D) After the noon prayer

Key Takeaway
Departing to Arafat after sunrise on the 9th is the recommended Sunnah; earlier departure is valid but less preferred.

Khutbah Before Prayer in Arafat: Hanafi vs Maliki
Ruling on combined prayer with inter-madhhab dispute

Learning Objective
By the end of this lesson, you will be able to state the Hanafi sequence of khutbah and prayer in Arafat, explain the Maliki objection, and identify the Hanafi response and mufta bihi ruling.

Core Idea
In Arafat, the khutbah teaches the rituals before the prayer; thus it must come first.

This lesson examines a well-known inter-madhhab dispute regarding the sequence of the khutbah and the combined Zuhr and Asr prayer on the Day of Arafat. The Hanafi school, following the practice of the Prophet ﷺ, places the khutbah before the prayer, while Imam Malik argues it should be after, akin to the Eid khutbah. Understanding the rationale behind each position deepens appreciation for how each school derives rulings from the same sources.

Guided Path
1
Identify the act and ruling
Determine what act is being described (the combined prayer in Arafat) and the Hanafi hukm level for the sequence.
The sequence is sunnah muakkadah; the overall prayer is wajib.
2
State the Hanafi position and its proof
What does the Hanafi school say about the order? What dalil do they cite?
Proof: Prophetic practice and the purpose of teaching the rites.
3
Analyze the Maliki objection
What is Imam Malik's argument? How does he analogize the khutbah to Eid?
His qiyas: khutbah of exhortation resembles Eid, which comes after prayer.
4
Examine the Hanafi response
How do the Hanafis rebut the Maliki analogy? What is the distinctive purpose of this khutbah?
Response: main purpose is ta'lim al-manasik (teaching rites), which must precede the acts.
5
Note the intra-Hanafi ikhtilaf on adhan timing
What are the two reports from Abu Yusuf, and which is the mufta bihi?
The correct view: adhan after imam sits on pulpit, before khutbah.

Source Text
⚠ Extracted via Advanced OCR ∼97% accuracy, minor errors may remain — always verify against original Arabic books
قَالَ وَإِذَا زَالَتِ الشَّمْسُ يُصَلّى الْإِمَامُ بِالنَّاسِ الظُّهَرَ وَالْعَصْرَ فَيَبْتَدِيُّ بِالْخُطْبَةِ فَيَخْطُبُ خُطْبَةٌ يُعَلِّمُ فِيهَا النَّاسَ الوقوفَ بِعَرَفَةَ وَالْمُرْدَ لَفَةِ وَرَى الْحِمَارِ وَالتَّحْرَ وَالْحَلْقِ وَطَوافِ الزِيَارَةِ يَخْطُبُ حُطَبَتَيْنِ يَفْصِلُ بَيْنَهُمَا بِجَلْسَةٍ كَمَا فِى الْجُمُعَةِ هَكَذَا فَعَلَهُ رَسُولُ اللهِ صلى الله عليه وسلم وَقَالَ مَالِكِ يَخْطُبُ بَعْدَ الصَّلوة لأنَّهَا خُطْبَة وَعْطٍ وَتَذْكِير فَأَشْبَهَ خُطْبَةَ الْعِيدِ وَلَنَا مَارَوَيْنَا وَلِأَنَّ الْمَقْصُودَ مِنْهَا تَعِلِيمُ الْمَنَاسِ وَالْجَمْعُ مِنْهَا وَفِى ظَاهِرِ الْمَذْهَبِ إِذًا . صَعِدَ الإِمَامُ الْمِنْبَرَ فَجَلَسَ أَذَّنَ الْمُؤَذِّنُونَ كَمَا فِى الْجُمُعَةِ وَعَنْ أَبِى يُوسُفَ أَنَّهُ يُؤَذِّنُ قَبْلَ خُرُوجِ الإِمَامِ وَعَنْهُ أنَّه يُؤَذِّنُ بَعْدَ الْخُطْبَةِ وَالصَّحِيحُ مَا ذَكَرْنَا لِأَنَّ النَّبِيَّ عَلَيْهِ السَّلَامُ لَمَّا خَرَجَ وَاسْتَوَى عَلَى نَاقَتِهِ أَذَّنَ الْمُؤَذِنُونَ بَيْنَ يَدَيْهِ وَيُقِيمُ الْمُؤذِّنُ بَعْدَ الْفَرَاغِ مِنَ الْخُطْبَةِ لأَنَّهُ أوانُ الشَّرُوعِ فِى الصَّلوة فَأَشبَهَ الْجُمْعَةَ قَالَ وَيُصَلِّي بِهِمُ الظُّهْرَ وَالْعَصْرَ فِي وَقْتِ الظُّهْرِ بِأَذَانِ وَاقَامَتِيْن وَقَدْوَرَدَ النَّقْلُ الْمُسْتَفِيضُ بِاتِّفَاقِ الرُّوَاةِ بِالْجَمْعِ بَيْنَ الصَّلَاتَيْنِ وَفِيمَا رَوى جَابِرٌ أَنَّ النَّبِيَّ صَلَّاهُمَا بِاَذَانٍ وَاقَامَتَيْنِ ثُمَّ بَيَانُه أَنه يَوذَنُ للظهرِ وَيُقِيمُ
He said: When the sun has passed its zenith, the imam leads the people in Zuhr and Asr. He begins with the khutbah, and delivers a khutbah in which he teaches the people the standing at Arafat, Muzdalifah, stoning the Jamarat, sacrifice, shaving the head, and Tawaf al-Ziyarah. He delivers two khutbahs, separating between them with a sitting just as in Friday [prayer]. This is what the Messenger of Allah (peace be upon him) did. Malik said: He delivers the khutbah after the prayer, because it is a sermon of exhortation and reminder, so it resembles the Eid khutbah. Our proof is what we have narrated, and because the purpose of it is teaching the rituals and the combining [of prayers] is among them. According to the apparent [position] of the madhhab: When the imam ascends the pulpit and sits, the mu'adhdhins give the adhan as in Friday. And from Abu Yusuf: that he gives the adhan before the imam's departure; and from him [another report]: that he gives the adhan after the khutbah. The correct is what we have mentioned, because when the Prophet (peace be upon him) came out and settled on his she-camel, the mu'adhdhins gave the adhan before him. And the mu'adhdhin gives the iqamah after finishing the khutbah, because that is the time to begin the prayer, so it resembles Friday. He said: And he prays with them Zuhr and Asr in the time of Zuhr with one adhan and two iqamahs. The mutawatir transmission has come by agreement of narrators regarding combining the two prayers. In what Jabir narrated, the Prophet prayed them with one adhan and two iqamahs. Then its explanation: he gives the adhan for Zuhr and establishes [the iqamah].
Source pages p. 337

Commentary
This passage is a ruling combined with an inter-madhhab dispute. It comes from the matn of al-Quduri, which the Sharh explains. The text states the Hanafi position: on the 9th of Dhul Hijjah, at zawal (noon), the imam first delivers two khutbahs just like Jumu'ah, teaching the rites of Hajj (wuquf at Arafat, Muzdalifah, stoning, sacrifice, shaving, Tawaf al-Ziyarah). Then he prays Zuhr and Asr together in the time of Zuhr. This is based on the Prophet's practice. Imam Malik differs, arguing that the khutbah should be after prayer, like 'Eid, because it is a sermon of exhortation. The Hanafi response: the purpose is teaching the rituals, which must be before the prayer, and the combining itself is a ritual that needs instruction. The Sharh then discusses the adhan and iqamah. The apparent madhhab (zahir al-madhhab) is that the adhan is given after the imam sits on the pulpit, like Jumu'ah. There are two reports from Abu Yusuf: one says before the imam's exit, another after the khutbah. The correct (sahih) according to the author is the first, because the Prophet gave adhan before his sermon. The iqamah is given after the khutbah, just like Jumu'ah. The text concludes that the prayer is performed with one adhan and two iqamahs: one iqamah for Zuhr and another for Asr. This is based on the hadith of Jabir. The authority weight of this ruling is from Zahir al-Riwayah, as it aligns with the six books of Imam Muhammad, and the dispute with Malik is well-known.

Key Terms
جمع بین الصلاتین (jam' bayn al-salatayn): Combining two prayers, here Zuhr and Asr, at the time of the earlier prayer (zuhr).
ظاہر المذہب (zahir al-madhhab): The apparent or well-known position of the Hanafi school, based on the six books of Imam Muhammad.
اذان و اقامتین (adhan wa iqamatayn): One adhan for both prayers, followed by two separate iqamahs: one for Zuhr and one for Asr.

Key Terms from Source Passage

Checkpoint
According to the Hanafi madhhab, what is the correct sequence of actions in Arafat on the 9th of Dhul Hijjah?
A) Zuhr prayer, then khutbah, then Asr prayer
B) Khutbah, then combined Zuhr and Asr with one adhan and two iqamahs
C) Adhan, then prayer, then khutbah
D) Asr prayer first, then Zuhr

Key Takeaway
In Arafat, the Hanafi school requires the khutbah to precede the combined Zuhr and Asr prayer because its purpose is to teach the Hajj rites, unlike the Eid khutbah.

The Khutbah on Arafah: Before or After Zuhr?
Dispute on timing of Arafah khutbah

Learning Objective
By the end of this lesson, you will be able to explain why the Hanafi school holds that the Arafah khutbah is before Zuhr and evaluate the Maliki counter-argument.

Core Idea
The Arafah khutbah is before prayer because the Prophet's practice overrides analogy with Eid.

In this passage, the commentator presents a dispute between the Hanafi and Maliki schools regarding the timing of the khutbah on the Day of Arafah. The Hanafi school, following al-Quduri, states that the khutbah is delivered before the combined Zuhr and Asr prayer, while Imam Malik argues it should be after prayer. Understanding this dispute requires analyzing the proofs and the underlying legal purposes.

Guided Path
1
State the Hanafi ruling
Identify the Hanafi position: the khutbah is delivered before the combined Zuhr and Asr prayer at the time of Zuhr. Also note that it consists of two parts with a sitting in between, like Jumu'ah.
This is based on the practice of the Prophet (peace be upon him) as narrated by Jabir.
2
Identify the Maliki position and its proof
State Imam Malik's view that the khutbah is after the prayer. Understand his evidence: analogy (qiyas) with the Eid khutbah, which is delivered after the prayer because it is a sermon of admonition.
The Maliki school relies on the principle that similar acts have similar rulings.
3
Examine the Hanafi proof
The Hanafi school provides two proofs: (1) the explicit hadith of Jabir that the Prophet gave the khutbah before Zuhr in Arafah, and (2) the purpose of the khutbah: teaching the rituals of Hajj, which is better achieved before the prayer so that people can act upon the instruction.
The hadith of Jabir is a clear textual evidence (dalil naqli) that overrides analogy.
4
Analyze the Hanafi response
The Hanafi response refutes the Maliki analogy by distinguishing the purpose: Arafah khutbah is for teaching rituals (including the combined prayer), while Eid khutbah is for admonition. Thus, the timing differs. Additionally, an explicit hadith takes precedence over qiyas.
This demonstrates the Hanafi principle that textual evidence (nass) cannot be overridden by reasoning (qiyas) when the text is explicit.
5
Determine the thamarah al-khilaf
The practical consequence of this dispute is the sequence of actions on Arafah: Hanafis deliver khutbah first, then pray; Malikis pray first, then deliver khutbah. Both are considered valid in their respective schools.
This difference affects the actual practice of pilgrims but does not affect the validity of the Hajj.

Source Text
⚠ Extracted via Advanced OCR ∼97% accuracy, minor errors may remain — always verify against original Arabic books
تشریح صاحب قدوری نے فرمایا کہ نویں ذی الحجہ کو میدان عرفات میں زوال آفتاب کے بعد امام المسلمین یا اس کا نائب لوگوں کو ظہر و عصر دونوں نمازیں ظہر کے وقت میں ادا کرائے ۔ ترتیب یہ ہوگی کہ پہلے خطبہ پڑھے گا جس میں لوگوں کو افعال حج کی تعلیم دے گا ۔ جمعہ کی طرح دو خطبے ہوں گے اور دونوں خطبوں کے درمیان بیٹھ کر فصل کردے گا۔ یہی رسول اللہ صلى الله عليه وسلم کا معمول ہے۔ حضرت امام مالک نے فرمایا ہے کہ یوم عرفہ کا خطبہ نماز کے بعد ہے نہ کہ نماز سے پہلے ۔ امام مالک کی دلیل یہ ہے کہ یہ خطبہ وعظ ونصیحت کا خطبہ ہے۔ لہذا عیدین کے خطبہ کے مشابہ ہو گیا اور عیدین کا خطبہ چونکہ نماز کے بعد پڑھا جاتا ہے اس لئے یہ خطبہ بھی نماز کے بعد پڑھا جائے گا۔ ہماری دلیل وہ روایت ہے جس کی طرف حدیث جابر میں اشارہ کیا گیا ہے۔ اور حدیث جابر میں بصراحت مذکور ہے کہ آنحضرت صلى الله عليه وسلم نے عرفات میں نماز ظہر سے پہلے خطبہ دیا ہے۔ دوسری دلیل یہ ہے کہ میدان عرفات میں خطبہ سے مقصود مناسک حج کی تعلیم دینا ہے اور جمع بین الصلاتین بھی مناسک حج میں سے ہے۔ اور تعلیم کا مقصد نماز سے پہلے خطبہ دینے سے حاصل ہوگا نہ کہ بعد میں خطبہ دینے سے۔ اس لئے ہمارے نزدیک نماز ظہر سے پہلے خطبہ پڑھنے کا حکم دیا گیا ہے۔
Sahib Quduri said: On the 9th of Dhul Hijjah, after the sun passes the meridian in the plain of Arafat, the Imam of the Muslims or his deputy should lead the people in both Zuhr and Asr prayers at the time of Zuhr. The sequence is that he will first deliver a khutbah in which he teaches the people the rituals of Hajj. There will be two khutbahs like Friday, and he will separate between the two khutbahs by sitting. This was the practice of the Messenger of Allah (peace be upon him). Imam Malik said that the khutbah of the Day of Arafah is after the prayer, not before. Imam Malik's evidence is that this khutbah is a sermon of admonition and advice, so it is similar to the khutbah of the two Eids, and since the Eid khutbah is delivered after the prayer, this khutbah should also be delivered after the prayer. Our evidence is the narration indicated in the hadith of Jabir, and in the hadith of Jabir it is explicitly mentioned that the Prophet (peace be upon him) gave the khutbah in Arafat before Zuhr prayer. The second evidence is that the purpose of the khutbah in the plain of Arafat is to teach the rituals of Hajj, and combining the two prayers is also among the rituals of Hajj. The purpose of teaching is achieved by giving the khutbah before the prayer, not after. Therefore, in our view, it is commanded to deliver the khutbah before Zuhr prayer.
Source pages p. 338

Commentary
This passage from the commentary on al-Hidayah addresses the ruling of the khutbah on the Day of Arafah. It begins by stating the ruling from al-Quduri that the imam combines Zuhr and Asr at Zuhr time and delivers a khutbah first, two sermons with a sitting between them like Jumu'ah. Then it presents Imam Malik's opposing view that the khutbah is after prayer, drawing an analogy to Eid khutbahs. The Hanafi response provides two proofs: explicit hadith of Jabir that the Prophet gave khutbah before Zuhr, and the purpose of teaching which requires the khutbah before the prayer.

Key Terms
خطبہ (khutbah): The sermon delivered on the Day of Arafah before the combined Zuhr and Asr prayer, consisting of two parts with a sitting in between.

Key Terms from Source Passage

Checkpoint
According to the Hanafi school, when is the khutbah delivered on the Day of Arafah?
A) Before Zuhr prayer
B) After Zuhr prayer
C) Before Asr prayer
D) After both prayers

Key Takeaway
The Hanafi school prefers the khutbah before Zuhr in Arafah based on the explicit hadith of Jabir and the purpose of teaching rituals.

The Timing of Adhan in Arafah: Text and Qiyas
Intra-Hanafi dispute on adhan timing in Arafah

Learning Objective
By the end of this lesson, you will be able to state the Hanafi position on when the adhan is given in Arafah and explain why qiyas with Jumu'ah is preferred despite conflicting hadith.

Core Idea
The adhan in Arafah is given before the khutbah, by analogy with Jumu'ah, resolving conflicting narrations.

The timing of the adhan on the Day of Arafah is not merely a ritual detail; it involves weighing conflicting transmitted reports (riwayat) and applying analogical reasoning (qiyas). In this lesson, we examine the intra-Hanafi dispute between the apparent madhhab of Abu Hanifa and two narrations from Imam Abu Yusuf, along with the Maliki position. By understanding how the Hanafi school resolves the conflict, you will see the interplay between text and reason in Hanafi fiqh.

Guided Path
1
Identify the three positions
List the three views on when the adhan is given in Arafah as mentioned in the passage: (1) adhan after imam sits on minbar (before khutbah) – apparent madhhab; (2) adhan before imam emerges from tent – Abu Yusuf's first narration; (3) adhan after khutbah – Abu Yusuf's second narration and Imam Malik.
2
Understand the evidence for each
For the apparent madhhab: the practice of the Prophet (peace be upon him) when he mounted his camel and the muezzin gave adhan. For the after-khutbah view: the hadith of Jabir that Bilal gave adhan after the khutbah. For the before-emergence view: analogy with ordinary Zuhr adhan.
The before-emergence view is also a form of adhan before khutbah.
3
Recognize the textual conflict
The two hadith (Prophet’s practice vs. Jabir’s report) apparently contradict each other. This is a case of ta'arud (conflict) of texts.
4
Apply the Hanafi principle for conflict
When primary texts (nusus) conflict and neither is clearly stronger, the Hanafi method resorts to qiyas (analogy) with a similar established case. Here, the khutbah in Arafah is analogous to the Friday khutbah, where the adhan is given before the khutbah.
Qiyas is used as a fallback when direct textual evidence is inconclusive.
5
Derive the final sequence
Result: adhan before the khutbah (after imam sits), then khutbah, then iqamah, then combined Zuhr and Asr prayer. The iqamah is given after the khutbah because that is when the prayer begins, just as in Jumu'ah.

Source Text
⚠ Extracted via Advanced OCR ∼97% accuracy, minor errors may remain — always verify against original Arabic books
رہی یہ بات کہ عرفات میں مؤذن اذان کب دے۔ خطبہ سے پہلے یا خطبہ کے بعد۔ سو اس بارے میں ہمارے علماء کا ظاہر مذہب یہ ہے کہ امام جب منبر پر چڑھ کر بیٹھ جائے تو بیٹھ جانے کے بعد اذان دی جاتی ہے۔ امام ابو یوسف سے ایک راویت یہ ہے کہ امام کے خیمہ سے نکلنے سے پہلے اذان دی جائے۔ چنانچہ مؤذن جب اذان دے کر فارغ ہو جائے تب امام اپنے خیمہ سے نکلے ۔ کیونکہ یہ اذان نماز ظہر ادا کرنے کے لئے ہے جیسا کہ دوسرے ایام میں زوال آفتاب کے بعد ادا و ظہر کے لئے اذان دی جاتی ہے۔ پس جس طرح دوسرے ایام میں امام کے تشریف لانے سے پہلے اذان دی جاتی ہے اسی طرح عرفات میں بھی امام کے برآمد ہونے سے پہلے اذان دی جائے گی۔ امام ابو یوسف کی دوسری روایت یہ ہے کہ خطبہ کے بعد اذان دی جائے گی۔ اسی کے قائل امام مالک ہیں۔ اس روایت کی دلیل یہ ہے کہ حدیث جابر میں مذکور ہے کہ حضرت بلال نے عرفات میں خطبہ کے بعد اذان دی ہے لیکن صحیح مذہب وہی ہے جس کو ہم نے ذکر کیا۔ یعنی امام کے منبر پر بیٹھ جانے کے بعد اذان دی جائے کیونکہ حضور صلى الله عليه وسلم جب اپنے خیمہ سے نکل کر اپنی ناقہ پر تشریف فرما ہو گئے تو آپ کے رو بر دکھڑے ہو کر مؤذن نے اذان دی۔ ظاہر مذہب کے صحیح ہونے کی دلیل یہ بھی ہے کہ حدیث جابر تقاضا کرتی ہے کہ اذان خطبہ کے بعد دی جائے۔ اور یہ روایت تقاضا کرتی ہے کہ خطبہ سے پہلے دی جائے۔ پس تعارض کی وجہ سے دونوں روایتوں کو چھوڑ کر قیاس علی الجمعہ پر عمل کیا جائے گا۔ صاحب ہدایہ فرماتے ہیں کہ خطبہ سے فراغت کے بعد مؤذن اقامت کہے کیونکہ نماز شروع ہونے کا یہی وقت ہے۔ پس جس طرح خطبہ جمعہ کے بعد اقامت کہی جاتی ہے اسی طرح عرفات کے خطبہ کے بعد بھی نماز ظہر کے لئے اقامت کہی جائے گی۔
As for when the muezzin gives the adhan in Arafah—before or after the khutbah—the apparent madhhab of our scholars is that when the imam climbs the minbar and sits, the adhan is given after he sits. From Imam Abu Yusuf, there is one narration that the adhan is given before the imam emerges from his tent. So when the muezzin finishes the adhan, then the imam emerges from his tent. Because this adhan is for performing the Zuhr prayer, just as on other days the adhan is given after the sun passes the meridian for Zuhr. So just as on other days the adhan is given before the imam arrives, similarly in Arafah the adhan will be given before the imam emerges. The second narration from Imam Abu Yusuf is that the adhan will be given after the khutbah. Imam Malik also holds this view. The evidence for this narration is that in the hadith of Jabir it is mentioned that Bilal (may Allah be pleased with him) gave the adhan in Arafah after the khutbah. But the correct madhhab is the one we mentioned, i.e., the adhan is given after the imam sits on the minbar, because when the Prophet (peace be upon him) emerged from his tent and sat on his she-camel, the muezzin gave the adhan standing in front of him. Another evidence for the correctness of the apparent madhhab is that the hadith of Jabir requires that the adhan be given after the khutbah, and this narration requires that it be given before the khutbah. So due to the conflict, both narrations are set aside and analogy with Jumu'ah (Friday) is acted upon. The author of al-Hidayah says: After the completion of the khutbah, the muezzin gives the iqamah, because this is the time to begin the prayer. So just as after the Friday khutbah the iqamah is said, similarly after the khutbah of Arafah the iqamah for Zuhr prayer will be said.
Source pages p. 338

Commentary
This passage discusses the timing of the adhan on the Day of Arafah. There are three views: (1) The apparent madhhab (of Abu Hanifa) that adhan is given after the imam sits on the minbar (before khutbah). (2) Imam Abu Yusuf's first narration that adhan is given before the imam emerges from his tent (also before khutbah). (3) Imam Abu Yusuf's second narration and Imam Malik's view that adhan is given after the khutbah. The preferred view is the apparent madhhab: adhan is given before the khutbah. This is based on the practice of the Prophet and analogy with Jumu'ah. The iqamah is given after the khutbah.

Key Terms
اذان (adhan): The call to prayer given on the Day of Arafah before the combined prayer. Its timing is before the khutbah according to the relied-upon Hanafi view.
اقامت (iqamah): The second call to signal the start of the prayer; in Arafah, it is given after the khutbah.
قیاس (qiyas): Analogical reasoning; used here to resolve the conflict between two hadith by comparing Arafah to Jumu'ah.

Key Terms from Source Passage

Checkpoint
According to the Hanafi school, when is the adhan given on the Day of Arafah?
A) After the imam sits on the minbar, before the khutbah
B) After the khutbah, before the iqamah
C) Before the imam emerges from his tent
D) After the prayer

Key Takeaway
The Hanafi school resolves the textual conflict on adhan timing in Arafah by using qiyas with Jumu'ah, placing the adhan before the khutbah.

Combining Zuhr and Asr in Arafah: One Adhan, Two Iqamahs
Explains method and proof for combining prayers on Arafah

Learning Objective
By the end of this lesson, you will be able to state the Hanafi method for combining Zuhr and Asr on the Day of Arafah and identify the proof from the hadith of Jabir.

Core Idea
Combining Zuhr and Asr in Arafah requires one adhan and two iqamahs.

On the Day of Arafah, the imam leads both Zuhr and Asr prayers at the time of Zuhr. The method is specific: one adhan for Zuhr, then an iqamah for Zuhr, then another iqamah for Asr. This lesson examines the ruling and its proof from the sunnah.

Guided Path
1
Identify the act and its ruling
The act is combining Zuhr and Asr on the Day of Arafah. Determine the hukm level: is it fard, wajib, sunnah, etc.?
The passage indicates it is a sunnah practice, not obligatory.
2
Locate the dalil
The proof is a widely transmitted narration (naql mustafid) and specifically the hadith of Jabir. Identify the exact wording of the hadith quoted.
The hadith states: 'He prayed them both with one adhan and two iqamahs.'
3
Trace the wajh al-dalalah
How does the hadith prove the method? The explicit mention of 'one adhan and two iqamahs' shows the manner of combining.
The term 'bi-adhanin wa iqamatayn' is clear and unambiguous.
4
Understand the rationale
Why is Asr given only an iqamah and not a separate adhan? Because Asr is offered before its usual time, and all people are already gathered from the Zuhr adhan.
The iqamah alone suffices to inform the congregation of the start of Asr.
5
Note the cross-madhhab difference
While the method is agreed upon by all schools for Arafah, Hanafis restrict combining to Hajj only, unlike Shafi'is who allow it for travel.
This is a thamarah al-khilaf in the scope of combining.
